################################################################################################################
################################################################################################################
####### Idea Variation 2 Scripted Gui by flogi (optical stuff only)
################################################################################################################
################################################################################################################

########################################################
####### Ideagroup adm_1 Start
########################################################

iv2_gui_stat_name_adm_1 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_1_1 
			
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_1_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_1_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
	}
}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_1 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_1_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_1
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_1
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_1
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_show_adm_1 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_1_1 
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}	
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_1
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_adm_1_1 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_1_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {

				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no

			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_1

			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_1
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}		
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_name_adm_2 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_2_1 
			
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_2
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_2_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_2
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_2_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_2
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
	}
}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_2 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_2_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_2
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_2
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_2
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_2
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_2
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_2
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {

				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_2
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}	
		NOT = {
			OR = {

					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_2
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_2
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes

iv2_gui_stat_name_adm_3 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_3_1 
			
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_3_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_3_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_3
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
	}
}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_3 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_3_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_3
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_3
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_3
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_show_adm_3 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_3_1 
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_3
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_3
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}	
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_3
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_adm_3_1 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_3_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_3_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_3
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_4 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_4_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_4
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_4
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_4
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_4
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_4
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_4
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_11 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_11_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_11
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_11
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_11
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_11
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_11
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_11
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {

			}

				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_13

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_13 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_13_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_13
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_13
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_13
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_13
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_13
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_13
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_16 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_16_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_16
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_16
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_16
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_16
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_16
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_16
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}

					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_18

				}
			}			
		}
	}

		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_18
			value = 1
		}
	}

			}

					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_23
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_23
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_23
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

		OR = {
			has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_25_1 
			
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_25
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_25_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_25
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_25_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_25
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
	}
}

	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_25_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_25
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_25
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_25
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_25
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_25
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_25
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_28 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_28_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_28
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_28
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_28
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_28
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_28
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_28
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

			}

					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_30
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}

		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_30
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_32_1 
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_32
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_32
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}	
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_32
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_32
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_32
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_show_adm_32
			value = 1
		}
	}

	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_35_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_35
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_35
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_35
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_35
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_35
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_35
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}

					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_37

			value = 1
		}
	}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_40 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_40_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_40
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_40
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_40
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_40
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_40
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_40
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_42_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_42
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_42
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_42
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_42
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_42
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_42
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_44_1 
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_44
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_44
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}	
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_44
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_44
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_44
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_show_adm_44
			value = 1
		}
	}

	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_47_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_47
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_47
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_47
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_47
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_47
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_47
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

			has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_49_1 
			
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_49
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_49_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_49
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
			AND = {

				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_49
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}

	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_49_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_49
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_49
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_49
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_49
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_49
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_49
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_52 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_52_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_52
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_52
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_52
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_52
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_52
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_52
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_53
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_53_6
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_53
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_53
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_53
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}		
		}
	}

iv2_gui_stat_name_adm_54 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_54_1 
			
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_54
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_54_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_54
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_54_1 
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_54
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
	}
}

iv2_gui_stat_hide_adm_54 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_54_1 
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_54
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_54
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}		
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_54
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}	
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_54
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}			
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_54
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_hide_adm_54
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

iv2_gui_stat_show_adm_54 = {
	scope = country 		
	is_valid = {  
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_54_1 
			has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_54
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_54
				has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
			}
		}	
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_54
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_no
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = iv2_stat_show_adm_54
					has_variable = iv2_var_show_all_ig_statistics_yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		remove_variable = iv2_stat_hide_adm_54
		set_variable = {
			name = iv2_stat_show_adm_54
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}
